endingPicker = (out, totv, aa, quickstats) => {

    function setImage(url) {
        if(url == '' || url == null) return;
        let interval = setInterval(function () {
            img = document.getElementsByClassName("person_image")[0];
            if (img != null) {
                img.src = url;
                clearInterval(interval);
            }
        }, 50);
    }

    if(quickstats[0] == 538) {
        setImage("https://i.imgur.com/evC7vnS.gif");
        return `<p>  ACCEPTANCE SPEECH, 2025 <p>

You stare into the endless sea of faces as they shout your name. As the endless shouting roars on, you think about how no one knows what you did. Your team did their job, and they did it well. It doesn't stop. It doesn't end. It will never end. It can't end.

The confetti rains down like artificial snow, but you barely feel it. Your speech waits on the podium behind you. The words carefully crafted by your staff, by your operatives. They read like the culmination of a lifetime of public service. Of clean victories. Of transparency. Of trust. But thats a story for them, not for you. You smile, because that is what you must do. Your lips curl into that perfect politicians smile, teeth white, eyes wide, voice strong. They cheer louder, hungry for every word you havent said yet.

<p> <i> They don't love you. They love the story you sold them. <i> <p>

Ending: Secret



`;
    }
    if(quickstats[0] > 312) {
        setImage("https://i.imgur.com/KBL0kh6.jpeg");
        return `placeholderending
`;
    }
    if(quickstats[0] > 270) {
        setImage("https://i.imgur.com/KBL0kh6.jpeg");
        return `placeholderending`;
    }
    if(quickstats[0] < 270) {
        setImage("https://i.imgur.com/KBL0kh6.jpeg");
        return `placeholderending`;
    }
    if(quickstats[0] < 160) {
        setImage("https://i.imgur.com/KBL0kh6.jpeg");
        return `placeholderending`;
    }
}
